ARIE 1918-1919 [vol. 041]


A.--List of copper-plates examined during the year 1918-19.


ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/1 (page 14)
Placement
The District Munsiff of Amba-samudram (Tinnevelly district).
Dynasty
Nāyaka
King
Vijayaraṅga-Chokkanātha-Nāyaka, son of Raṅga-Kṛishṇa-Muttuvīrappa-Nā-yaka and grandson of Chok-kanātha-Nāyaka.
Date
Śaka 1617, Kollam 871, Āḍi 11, śu. di. daśamī, Thursday, Anusham.
Language
Tamil
Origin
…
Edition
…
Remarks
Records sarvamānya grants of Vāgaikuḷam, Śeṅguḷam, Aviśāgappēri, Arppanāṅguḷam, belonging to the north-east hamlet of Rāja-rāja-chaturvēdimaṅgalam, Iluppaikkuṟich-chi, and others, made by a Pāṇḍya king in Śaka 1408, corresponding to Kollam 661, Puraṭṭādi 20, ba. di. saptamī, Tuesday, Mṛi-gaśīrsha and during the reigns of Mallikār-juna, Virūpāksha, Kṛishṇarāya and Vīra-mārtāṇḍa, for daily worship, monthly and annual festivals, offerings and other require-ments, to the temple of Nayinār-Nāṟumpūṅ-koṇḍaruḷiya-Tambirāṉār at Dakshiṇakāśi alias Puṭārjunasthaḷa, in Muḷḷi-nāḍu.

ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/3 (page 14)
Placement
M.R.Ry. Chilukuri Narayana Rao Garu, M.A., L.T., Teacher, Chicacole (Ganjam district).
Dynasty
Eastern Gaṅga.
King
Vajrahasta III
Date
Śaka 97[1] Karkaṭaka, Śukla-paksha Trayōdaśī, Sunday.
Language
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
In the Epigra-phia Indica by Messrs. G.V.Rama-murthi Pan-tulu and Chi-lukūri Nara-yana Rao.
Remarks
Records the gift of the village Sattivāḍa in E1rada-vishaya, to Gaṇapati-Nāyaka, the grandson of Gaṇapati, a resident of the village Valutavūru in Kaṁchidēśa.
ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/4 (page 14)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Dēvēndravarmman Rājarāja-dēva, son of Vajrahasta III and Anaṅga-Mahādēvī.
Date
Śaka 998, Chaitra, Vishu-Saṅ-krānti.
Language
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
In the Epigra-phia Indica by Messrs. G.V.Rama-murthi Pan-tulu and Chi-lukūri Nara yana Rao.
Remarks
Records the gift of the village Vṛihat-Koḍila in Varāhavarttanī, to Vāsudēvaśarman of the Vatsa-gōtra and Nārāyaṇaśarman of the Kāśyapa-gōtra, who were residents of the village Kalipure. The king was crowned in Śaka 992, on Jēshṭha, Śubhra, Ashṭamī, Siṁha-lagna, Thursday with Uttara-Phal-gunī.
ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/5 (page 14)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Madhukā[m]ārṇavadēva, son of Anantavarma.
Date
526th year of the Gaṅga rule.
Language
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
In the Epigra-phia Indica by Messrs. G.V.Rama-murthi Pan-tulu and Chi-lukūri Nara yana Rao.
Remarks
States that the three villages Paṭugrāma, Hoṇḍaravaḍo and Morakhiṇi were together formed into a Vaiśya-agrahāra and granted to a certain Erapa-Nāyaka, the son of Mañchi-Nāyaka of the Vaiśya caste.
ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/6 (page 14)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Anantavarman-Chōḍagaṅga-dēva, son of Rājarāja and Rājasundarī.
Date
Śaka 1006
Language
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
In the Epigra-phia Indica by Messrs. G.V.Rama-murthi Pan-tulu and Chi-lukūri Nara yana Rao.
Remarks
Registers the gift of the village of Sellada in the [Rū]pāvarttani-vishaya, to Komarachan-dra, son of Nannipāṅgu and grandson of Vallanapāṅgu, a resident of Talāgrāma, for worship, offerings and lamps of the goddess Bhagavatī of that (i.e., Sellada) village and for the repair of the temple.

ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/9 (page 15)
Placement
The Collector of Nellore
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Kanarese
Origin
Will be acquired for the Govern-ment Museum as Treasure Trove.
Edition
…
Remarks
States that the five hundred Svāmis of Ayyā-vuḷa granted as sarvamānya, the exemption of the tolls, suṅka, magame and bīraṇa, on 50 packages on bullocks, buffaloes or assess to a certain Malli-Seṭṭi, for having construc-ted the temple of Gannapēśvara at Nellūri-paṭṭaṇa surnamed Abhinava-Dvārāvatī and Chikk-Ayyāvoḷe.
ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/10 (page 15)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1225, Krōdhi, Kār-tika, śu. di. 10, Thurs-day.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Will be acquired for the Govern-ment Museum as Treasure Trove.
Edition
…
Remarks
Grant of the privilege to trade in certain articles without paying duty, to a certain Puliyama-Seṭṭi for having killed Kārapāka-la Kāṭi-Nāyaka who had become a traitor to the samayas, by the merchants of the eigh-teen samayas of all countries (residing) in Nandyāla-sthala.
ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/11 (page 15)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Kākatīya
King
Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Pratāpa-Rudradēva-Mahārāja, ruling at O1ruṅgallu.
Date
Śaka 1244, Dundubhi, Kārttika, śu. di. 5. Thurs-day.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Will be acquired for the Govern-ment Museum as Treasure Trove.
Edition
…
Remarks
Records a grant similar to the above by the same body of merchants to a certain Attena, son of Lōki-Seṭṭi for having killed Annama-rāja and Siṅgarāja the suṅka-karaṇas (toll-accountants) of Cheṟunūru in Peḍakaṇṭi-dēśa.
ARIE/1918-1919/A/1918-19/12 (page 15)
Placement
The Deputy Collector of Atmakur, Nellore district.
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Kṛishṇadēva-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1448, Vyaya, Vaiśākha, śu. di. Pūrṇimā.
Language
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Origin
Returned
Edition
…
Remarks
Only the second and last plates of the set are available. Records a grant of the village Koṇḍavāśali or Bhaṇḍāra Penuparti sur-named Kṛishṇadēva-Mahārāyasamudra in Rāpūru-sīma which belonged to the Nellūru-vaḷita in the Udayāchala-rājya to a number of Brahmans whose names are not given in the record.

B.--Stone inscriptions copied in 1918.


COIMBATORE DISTRICT


KOLLEGAL TALUK


ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/196 (page 16)
Placement
On a slab set up near the Māram-man temple at Tagarapuram.
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Kṛishṇavarmma-Mahādhirāya [i.e., Kṛi-shṇadēva-Mahārāya].
Date
Śaka 1437, Bhāva, Chaitra, ba. di. 5, Friday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers the grant of the village Tagavūru to Sōmayya-dēva-Oḍeya, son of Bāloḍeya of Mōgūru by Sāḷuva-Gōvindarāja with the consent of his younger brother the Mahāpradhāna (prime minister) Sāḷuva Timmarasa, under the orders of the king. The king is stated to be the son of Kaṭhāri-Sāḷuva Nārasiṁhavarma-Mahārāja, the lord of the Southern Ocean. The donee's grand-father Sōmēśvarāchārya, also called Mallikārjuna, was the guru of Vīra-Rudra, the lord of the town of O1ruṅ-gallu.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/197 (page 16)
Placement
On a stone oil-mill set up in a field near the same village.
Dynasty
Hoysaḷa
King
Vī[ra]-Ballāḷadēva
Date
Bhāva, Srashṭhi, (Jyēshṭha), ba. di. 9, Jīvavāra [i.e., Friday].
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Gives the names of several persons that set up a nandi-pillar and an oil-mill. On the reverse is given the name of Sōmaṇṇa the son of Belāḷadēva (i.e., the king ?).
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/198 (page 16)
Placement
On a slab lying by the side of the road from Kollegal to Mudi-gundam.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Fragment. Refers to a tax-free dēvadāna, to the temple of ... ṇḍīśvaramuḍaiyār Pe[ri]yadēśa-Nāyaka (by a resident ?) of Koḷḷakk[āl].
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/199 (page 16)
Placement
On a broken hero-stone lying near the Uttamamman temple at Lokkanahalli.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Records that a certain Kōdaṇḍa knocked down his own head and died. Mention is made of a certain Rāchamma and his wife Rā[jabe].
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/200 (page 16)
Placement
On a stone lying near the same temple.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
In archaic characters. This is the nisidhi set up by Dōramma in memory of his father Jaigevaḷe Basavayya who took the sanyāsa and fulfilled the four vows.

BELLARY DISTRICT


HARAPANAHALLI TALUK


ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/201 (page 16)
Placement
On a slab set up near the Āñjanē-yasvāmin temple at Nāndi-Be-vuru.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Trailōkyama[Iladēva]
Date
Śaka 976, Jaya, Uttarāyaṅa-Saṅ-rānti, Sunday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers that while Trailōkyamalla-Noḷamba-Pallava-Permanaḍi was ruling the No[ḷambavāḍi] 32,000, Balla-kunde [300] and Kodambaḷi 1,000, the 120 mahājanas of Rēchchūru, granted for the worship of Jina, a garden, a wet field, 5 houses and one oil-mill, to a certain Ashṭō-pavāsi-Bhaḷa of Dēsiga-Gaṇa. The record mentions Jagadēkamalla-Noḷamba-Brahmādhirāja as a subordinate of the chief mentioned above. On the back of the slab is a partly damaged record of the same period, referring to a grant made to Ashṭōpavāsi-muni at Baihūru. A certain Vīranandi-siddhānti is mentioned.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/202 (page 16)
Placement
On a beam of the Kallēśvarasvā-min temple in the same village.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1480, Kāḷa-yukti, Vaiśākha, ba. di. 12.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers the grant of the village Nandiya-Bēvūru for lamps to the temple of Lakshmīnārāyaṇa of the same village. The gift was made for the merit of Bhikshā-vṛitti-Ayya by his agent Vīrapa-Oḍeya Immaḍi Oḍeya.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/203 (page 16)
Placement
On a slab lying in a field to the north of the same village.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Nandana, Mārga-śira, ba. di. 12, Friday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers gift of land to a private individual by the Mahā-janas and others for the construction of a car to the temple of Basavaṇṇa.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/204 (page 17)
Placement
On a pillar in the madhya-maṇḍapa of the Pampāpatisvāmin temple at Bennehalli.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
…
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers gift of lands in the villages Hoḷagundhe, Moriṅ-gere, and Rājana-Beṇṇevūru, by the Mahāmaṇḍalāchār-ya Khaḷēśvaradēva, the rājaguru (the royal teacher) to the tammaḍis (Śiva-worshippers). The donor is said to have propagated the new Pāśupata-samaya and to have been the President of the 77 (?) (saptāhattari) sthānas and the chakravarti of the 7 crore samayas of Kōgaḷi 500.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/205 (page 17)
Placement
On another pillar in the same temple.
Dynasty
Yādava
King
Yādavanārāyaṇa Bhujabaḷa Prauḍha-Pratāpachakravartin Vīra-Rāmachan-dradēva.
Date
10th year, Pra-mādhi, Phālguṇa śu. ekādaśī, Monday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Records the gift of 18 gadyāṇas of money and 1 mattar of land by the rājaguru Vubhaṇa Yitavāhi (i.e., Hitavāhi ?) dēva-Rāṇeya to the 12 mahājanas of the agrahāra of Byaṁṇayahaḷi for a water-shed in the santhe (i.e., market place).
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/206 (page 17)
Placement
On a pillar in the front maṇḍapa of the same temple.
Dynasty
…

Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Vīra-Pāṇḍyadēva, ‘ruling at Uchchaṅgi’.
Date
Īśvara
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Damaged. Registers the gift of the village of Beṇṇevūru to the temple of Virūpāksha.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/207 (page 17)
Placement
On another pillar in the same maṇḍapa.
Dynasty
Hoysaḷa
King
Pratāpachakravartin Vīra-Baḷḷāḷadēva
Date
Piṅgaḷa, amāvāsya, Monday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers the gift of the tax mūligadeṟe, the taxes on looms, oil mills, the five artisan classes and the taxes on the minor communities, by Uttarāka-Heggaḍe and Janayya-Heggaḍe for offerings and for feeding Brāhmaṇas in the temple of Virūpākshadēva.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/208 (page 17)
Placement
On the same slab
Dynasty
Do.
King
Yādavanārāyaṇa Pratāpachakravartin Vīra-Nārasiṁhadēva.
Date
Chitrabhānu, Bhādrapada, ba. di. ashṭamī, Thursday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers the gift of a cow and a buffalo, for offerings and lamps and for feeding 12 mahājanas in the temple of Virūpākshadēva at Bāṇāvūru, by Giripayya Piriyaṇṇa, the keeper (ugrāṇi) of the good buffaloes.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/209 (page 17)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Do.
Date
Chitrabhānu, Bhādrapada, amā-vāsya, Monday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Seems to record a gift to the temple of Virūpāksha at Beṇṇevūru by the members of the district assembly (mahā-nāḍu) among whom were heggaḍes and sāmantas.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/210 (page 17)
Placement
On a slab set up in the same temple.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Pratāpachakravartin Jagadēkamalladēva
Date
11th year, Śukla Chaitra, śu. amāvāse, Monday, Uttarāyaṇa-saṅkrānti.
Language
Kanarese (prose & verse)
Remarks
Records that the Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Jagadēkamalla Vīra-Pāṇḍyadēva, ruling the Noṇambavāḍi 32,000 from his capital Uchchaṅgi, granted a vṛitti to the 12 Brāhmaṇas of the brahmapuri (Brahman village) of Beṇṇeganūru, to the asceties, etc., of the temple of Svayambhudēva at the village, while over the Koṭṭūru 12 and Kōgaḷi 500, the Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Nāchidevarasa, lord of Banavāsi was ruling from Koṭṭūru. Mentions in succession the Abhinava-Pāśupata teachers Lakuḷīśa, Vidyārāśi-Paṇḍita, Dharmarāśi-Paṇḍita and Chandrarāśi the contemporary of the donor.

ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/213 (page 18)
Placement
On a slab set up near the Kallēś-varasvāmin temple at Kuruvatti.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Ch. Vik. 24, Pra-mādhi, Jēshṭa, śu. Paurṇamāsi, Sunday, Lunar eclipse.
Language
Kanarese (prose & verse)
Remarks
Registers grant of land and taxes on grass, firewood, vegetables, fruits and cotton exported to and imported from Kuruvatti together with money for offerings, festivals and incense and for feeding asceties in the temple of Abhinava-Sōmēśvara by two hundred great men of the village and Kāḷidāsa, its chief. The village belonged to the Beṇṇevūru 12 which was ruled by Surēśvara-Paṇḍita-dēva. Lakuḷīśvara-Paṇḍita whose santāna, i.e., spiritual descent is given in the record was present at the ceremony of grant.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/214 (page 18)
Placement
On a slab set up in the Mallikārju-nasvāmin temple in the same village.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva, ‘ruling at the capital Kalyāṇapura.’
Date
Ch. Vik. 29, Tāra-ṇa, Vaiśākha, śu. tadige, Sunday.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
States that the mahājanas of the agrahāra Gaṇḍarādityana-Hoḻalu, having comaplained to the emperor (chakravarti) that Manneya Boppaya who captured Hoḻalu was plunder-ing all properties and killing the Brāhmaṇas in the village, the emperor sent for Boppaya, chastised him and took from him an undertaking that he and his successors should secede from the government of Hoḻalu. The chief did accordingly in the presence of the thirty-two thousand (representatives) of Beṇṇevūru 12, Nīrugunda 2, Haḍaṅ-gili, Māṅgoḷa, Bidirahaḷḷi, Hāhanūru, Honnavatti, Kuṟu-vatti and Bāḻguḷi and drank water at the temple of Tri-purāntakadēva.
ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/215 (page 18)
Placement
On a beam in the same temple
Dynasty
Gutta
King
Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Vikramādityadēva, ‘lord of Ujjenipura.’
Date
Śaka 1104, Plava, Pushya, ba. di. 3, Friday, Saṅkra-maṇa.
Language
Kanarese
Remarks
Records that, while the chief was governing the Beḷuhuge 70 and Beṇṇevūru 12, his minister (pradhāna) Susaga-Daṇṇāyaka, on the sanction of the Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Vijaya-Pāṇḍyarasa, renewed, in the presence of the mahā-janas of Kuṟuvatti and Bācharasa of Beṇṇeyūru, the grant of 70 mattar of lands originally made to the temple of Āhavamallēśvara by the elder (hiriya) Vikramāditya.

ARIE/1918-1919/B/1918/410 (page 35)
Placement
On the south wall of the central shrine in the Tiruttāḷamuḍaiyār temple at Tirukkolakkal.
Dynasty
Chōḷa
King
Tribhuvanachakravartin Tirubhuvana-vīradēva, ‘who having taken Madura and Īḻam (Ceylon), ......’ was pleased to perform the anointment of heroes and victors.
Date
3[5]th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Built in at the end. Seems to record that owing to the default made by a person who held the land belonging to the temple of Tirukkōlakkāvuḍaiya-Nāyanār in Tirukkaḻumala-nāḍu, the income was found to be in-sufficient to meet the expenses of the temple for the second half-year and that the land was re-sold in favour of a fresh tenant for an increased rate of rent.

ARIE/1918-1919/C/1919/8 (page 48)
Placement
On the north and west walls of the central shrine in the Vishṇu temple at Dadapuram (Tindi-vanam taluk, same district).
Dynasty
Chōḷa
King
Rājakēsarivarman alias Rājarājadēva
Date
21st year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Gives a list of vessels and ornaments made of gold, silver and pearls and presented to the temples of Kundavai-Viṇṇagar, Iravikulamāṇikka-Īśvara and Kundavai-Jinā-laya, built by the princess Parāntakaṉ Kundavai-piraṭṭi-yār, daughter of Poṉmāḷigaittuñjinadēvar, in the city of Rājarājapuram in Nallūr-nāḍu, a sub-division of Veṇ-kuṉṟa-kōṭṭam. Mentions the office Parākramaśōḻa-Mū-vēndavēḷār.

ARIE/1918-1919/C/1919/17 (page 49)
Placement
On the north and west walls of the central shrine in the Māṇikyēśva-rasvāmin temple in the same village.
Dynasty
Chōḷa
King
Rājakēsarivarman alias Rājarājadēva
Date
21st year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Refers to the construction of the 3 temples at Rājarājapuram mentioned in No. 8 above, by princess Pirāntakaṉ Kundavi-Pirāṭṭiyār and records that on receipt of the royal writ the officer Ārūraṉ Aravaṇaiyāṉ alias Parākra-maśōḻa-Mūvēndavēḷāṉ of Paṉaiyūr, in Iḷaiyūr-nāḍu a sub-division of Vēśālippāḍi, ordered the temple treasury to be examined and the presents made engraved on stone in the respective temples. The presents consisted of vessels and ornaments of various descriptions, made of gold, silver and pearl.

ARIE/1918-1919/C/1919/28 (page 50)
Placement
On the west and south walls of the same shrine.
Dynasty
Chōḷa
King
Rājarāja-Rājakēsarivarman
Date
17th year
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Records that the officer Ārūraṉ Udaiyadivākaraṉ Arumoḻi-Mūvēndavēḷāṉ of Araiśūr while stationed at Paṭṭaṉam in Paṭṭaṉa-nāḍu, a subdivision of O1ymā-nāḍu, received a complaint that the expenses of the temple of Bhumīśvara-dēva were not conducted since the grant of the dēvadāna of Manakkāṉam and fixed a fresh scale of expenses after due enquiry. States that the birth-day asterism (tirunAL) of king Rājarājadēva was Śadaiyan.

44th year
Language
Tamil
